-      <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)"><div class="sp-faq-q">What budget do I need for Google Ads? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div><div class="sp-faq-a">We recommend a minimum of Γé╣20,000ΓÇôΓé╣30,000/month in ad spend. Management fees are separate from ad spend.</div></div>
-      <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)"><div class="sp-faq-q">Can you take over my existing Google Ads account? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div><div class="sp-faq-a">Yes ΓÇö we do this often. We start with a full account audit to understand what's working, what's wasting spend, and what's missing.</div></div>
-      <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)"><div class="sp-faq-q">How is Performance Max different from Search? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div><div class="sp-faq-a">Search targets specific keywords. Performance Max uses AI to serve ads across all Google surfaces. PMax works best with strong creative assets and clear conversion data. We recommend running both.</div></div>
-      <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)"><div class="sp-faq-q">How quickly can campaigns go live? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div><div class="sp-faq-a">Typically 14ΓÇô21 days from onboarding to launch ΓÇö including audit, keyword research, ad copy, tracking setup, and campaign build.</div></div>

+          <div class="sp-faq-a">We write detailed creative briefs your team or a freelancer can execute. Our focus is
+            strategy, targeting, and performance ΓÇö not video production.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">What is CAPI and why does it matter? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">CAPI (Conversions API) is server-side tracking that sends conversion data directly from
+            your server to Meta ΓÇö bypassing iOS14 browser restrictions. Without it, you lose 30ΓÇô60% of your conversion
+            signals.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">How long before I see results? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Most campaigns exit the learning phase in 7ΓÇô14 days. Meaningful CPL improvement
+            typically happens within 3ΓÇô5 weeks. Unlike SEO, Meta can generate leads within 48 hours of going live.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Do you manage both Facebook and Instagram? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Yes ΓÇö both run through Meta Ads Manager. We allocate budget across placements based on

+    <!-- FAQs -->
+    <section class="sec">
+      <div class="sh">
+        <div class="stag">FAQs</div>
+        <h2 class="stitle">Common CRO questions.</h2>
+      </div>
+      <div class="sp-faq-list">
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">How much traffic do I need for CRO to work? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">You need enough traffic to reach statistical significance ΓÇö typically 500ΓÇô1,000
+            conversions per variant per test. For lower-traffic sites, we focus on qualitative methods first (heatmaps,
+            session recordings, UX review) and make high-confidence changes before running formal A/B tests.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">How long does a CRO test take to run? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Most tests run for 2ΓÇô4 weeks to collect enough data across different traffic patterns
+            and days of the week. We never call a test early ΓÇö even if one variant looks like it's winning ΓÇö until we
+            reach 95%+ statistical confidence.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Do you redesign the whole page or make targeted changes? <span
+              class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Both, depending on what the data shows. Sometimes a single headline change doubles
+            conversions. Sometimes the page structure itself is the problem. We let user behaviour data guide the scope
+            ΓÇö never our assumptions about what looks nice.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Can CRO run alongside our existing ad campaigns? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span>
+          </div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Absolutely ΓÇö and it's most powerful when it does. Improving your landing page conversion
+            rate means every rupee you spend on ads delivers more results. A 40% lift in CVR is the same as cutting your
+            CPL by 40%, without touching your bids.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">What if a test produces no clear winner? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">An inconclusive test is still valuable ΓÇö it tells us that particular variable isn't the
+            bottleneck. We document the learning, move on to the next highest-impact hypothesis, and continue the cycle.
+            No test is wasted.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Will this work with our existing website platform? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span>
+          </div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Yes ΓÇö CRO tools like Hotjar, Clarity, and VWO work across all major platforms including
+            WordPress, Webflow, Shopify, custom builds, and landing page builders. We assess your setup during
+            onboarding and confirm compatibility before starting.</div>
+        </div>
+      </div>

+    <section class="sec">
+      <div class="sh">
+        <div class="stag">FAQs</div>
+        <h2 class="stitle">Common Analytics questions.</h2>
+      </div>
+      <div class="sp-faq-list">
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">My GA4 is already set up ΓÇö why do I need this? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Most GA4 setups we audit are tracking less than 70% of actual conversions ΓÇö missing
+            events, double-counting sessions, or firing tags incorrectly. "Set up" and "set up correctly" are very
+            different things. We audit first and show you exactly what's missing before starting any work.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Do you need access to our website code? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Usually not ΓÇö Google Tag Manager handles most tracking changes without touching your
+            code. We'll need GTM admin access and GA4 property access. For custom events (e.g. SPA apps or e-commerce
+            data layers), we may need brief developer collaboration.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">What's in the monthly performance reports? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Each report covers: channel performance vs previous period, conversion trends, top and
+            bottom performing campaigns, funnel drop-off points, and 3ΓÇô5 specific recommendations for the next 30 days.
+            Written in plain English ΓÇö no jargon, no vanity metrics.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Can you connect our CRM data to GA4? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">Yes ΓÇö and this is one of the highest-value things we do. By importing qualified lead and
+            revenue data from your CRM back into GA4, we can show which campaigns and keywords actually drove customers
+            ΓÇö not just clicks. This makes every future ad decision far more accurate.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Is this a one-time setup or an ongoing retainer? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span>
+          </div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">We offer both. The initial setup is a one-time engagement (7ΓÇô14 days). Ongoing retainers
+            include monthly reports, dashboard maintenance, new event tracking as your site evolves, and quarterly
+            deep-dive analysis. Most clients start with setup and move to ongoing.</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="sp-faq-item" onclick="toggleFaq(this)">
+          <div class="sp-faq-q">Which channels can you track and attribute? <span class="sp-faq-icon">+</span></div>
+          <div class="sp-faq-a">All of them ΓÇö Google Ads, Meta Ads, organic search, email, direct, referral, and any
+            other channel you run. We set up cross-channel attribution models so you see how channels work together
+            across the full customer journey, not just last-click credit.</div>
+        </div>
